"rd_so_tips_drone"		"IAF情况说明单：\n• 爪虫只能用爪子攻击。 在它们到达小队之前干掉它们，就会让它们变得无害。 \n• 众所周知，某些爪虫可以飞跃很远的距离。 使用爆炸性武器时要格外小心，因为目标可能会迅速进入不安全范围。 \n• 爪虫可以在管道和脚手架下爬行。 有时可以封锁爪虫的出口，将它们困在一个不会对士兵们构成威胁的地方。"
"[english]rd_so_tips_drone"		"IAF Fact Sheet:\n• Drones only attack with their claws. Taking them out before they reach the squad will render them harmless.\n• Certain drones have been known to leap large distances. Take extra precautions when using explosive weaponry, as targets may rapidly advance into unsafe range.\n• Drones can crawl through ducts and under scaffolding. It is sometimes possible to block the drones' points of egress, trapping them in a location where they are not a threat to marines."
"rd_so_tips_ranger"		"IAF情况说明单：\n• 喷射虫的酸性武器以固定的高度飞行。翻滚闪避出弹道线，以干净利落地逃脱。\n• 喷射虫无法近战攻击。接近喷射虫的唯一风险就是被一颗近距离的酸球击中。\n• 喷射虫开火时不能转身。可利用这个机会到侧翼或者进入近战范围。"
"[english]rd_so_tips_ranger"		"IAF Fact Sheet:\n• The ranger's acidic weapon travels at a constant height. Dodge roll out of the way for a clean escape.\n• Rangers lack a melee attack. The only risk in getting close to a ranger is a point-blank acid orb.\n• Rangers cannot turn while firing. Use this opportunity to flank or get into melee range."
"rd_so_tips_shieldbug"		"IAF情况说明单：\n• 盾虫前面的大骨板是完全刀枪不入的。从侧边或通过缝隙攻击才能造成伤害。\n• 盾虫有两种姿势。“进攻型”姿态移动和转弯更快，但降低了骨板的覆盖。“防御性”姿态移动和转弯速度变慢，以获取了盾牌的合并。\n• 盾虫在受伤时经常切换到防御姿势。通常最好是在试图从侧翼攻击它之前先射击它，以利用它降低的移动速度。"
"[english]rd_so_tips_shieldbug"		"IAF Fact Sheet:\n• The large bone plates on the front of a shieldbug are completely invulnerable. Attack from the side or through gaps to do damage.\n• Shieldbugs have two stances. The \"offensive\" stance moves and turns faster, but reduces coverage from the bone plates. The \"defensive\" stance moves and turns slower in exchange for having its shields up.\n• Shieldbugs often switch to defensive stance when injured. It's often best to shoot one before attempting to flank to take advantage of its reduced movement speeds."

"rd_so_paragraph_drone_0"		"03/28/43，15:23\n我认为我们永远无法真正理解这些。 关于它们的形态、它们的行为，甚至它们来自哪里，我们还有很多要研究的。 我们所知道的一切都是以巨大的人命代价换来的。 我记录了近五十种相同体型的不同变化。 如果算上我直接证实的变异，那就是三倍。 我一直在整理关于爪虫迅速变异的惊人新功能，以及外壳颜色的传闻。 即使其中有一半是真的，我担心我们可能永远无法将所有可能的变异分类，更别用说想一劳永逸地消灭这种癌症了。"
"[english]rd_so_paragraph_drone_0"		"03/28/43, 15:23\nI don't think we'll ever truly understand these. There's so much to learn about their morphology, their behavior, even where they came from. Everything we do know came at a great human cost. I've recorded nearly fifty different variations on the same body plan. Triple that if you include the mutations I've confirmed firsthand. I've been trying to assemble the scant rumors of drones rapidly mutating astonishing new capabilites and carapace coloration. If even half of these are true, I worry we may never be able to catalog every possible variation, much less stamp this cancer out once and for all."
"rd_so_paragraph_drone_1"		"04/03/43, 08:14\n它们不是天然的。 即使它们在某种程度上算是一个进化物种，但有证据表明，这是一些实验将一些现有的生物，变成了这些能摧毁殖民地的寄生虫。 这在很大程度上解释了它们显著的基因多样性。 如果唯一的共同先祖是某种实验性寄生虫，那就意味着无论是什么怪物创造了这些东西，都想为它们的病态实验体找到最好的宿主。 如果人类活动假说能带来一线希望，那就是我们能找到治愈的方法。 这既是为了我们也是为了它们。 我必须相信我们还有机会治愈银河系里的这群外星异形。 肯定有比让IAF冒着生命危险，在所有人都死了几周后，再去引爆炸弹的更好办法。"
"[english]rd_so_paragraph_drone_1"		"04/03/43, 08:14\nThey aren't natural. Even if they were an evolved species at some point, there's evidence of experiments turning some existing being into these colony-destroying parasites. This goes a long way to explaining their remarkable genetic diversity. If the only common ancestor is some experimental parasite, it means whatever monsters created these things wanted to find the best possible hosts for their sick experiments. If the anthropogenic hypothesis offers one ray of hope, it's that we can find some kind of cure. Both for our sake and theirs. I have to believe there's still a chance to cure the galaxy of this alien swarm. There's got to be a better way than risking IAF lives and detonating stations after every last human's been dead for weeks."
"rd_so_paragraph_drone_2"		"04/14/43, 20:42\n我一直在和斯洛瑞奥博士通信。 现在还不清楚我们是否可以互相信任，但她有一些有趣的数据。 她不是IAF的，但这也许是最好的结果。 我担心我对虫群的研究会限制我的职业生涯，尤其是在纳姆.霍姆纳发生那种事之后，但我必须知道。 如果我能证明它们来自哪里——无论它们来自哪个地方——就可能再也不会有人因为这些东西而死了。 也许有一天，我可以走在黑暗的走廊上时，不会听到幽灵从我肩上掠过。"
"[english]rd_so_paragraph_drone_2"		"04/14/43, 20:42\nI've been exchanging correspondence with Dr. Scenario. It's still early days while we figure out if we can trust each other, but she has some fascinating data. She's not IAF, but that may be for the best. I worry my research into the swarm is a career-limiting move, especially after what happened on Nam Humanum, but I have to know. If I can prove where they came from- if they came from anywhere at all- it's possible no one will ever have to die to these things again. Perhaps one day, I'll be able to walk down a dark hallway without hearing phantom skittering over my shoulder."
"rd_so_paragraph_drone_3"		"04/20/43, 18:35\n赫维提卡很有道理。 我想我在IAF的日子屈指可数了。她答应在“办公室”给我一个职位——但她不会告诉我那是什么意思。 如果这是一个我可以研究虫群，并能得到一些实际支持的地方，那我将毫不迟疑地跳槽。 唯一的问题是，当我的直觉告诉我，我现在处于全局最大值时，我是否应该相信。 我做的每一步都有可能是错误的。 我不知道我是在跟魔鬼做交易，还是从沉船上获取救生圈，还是被人盯上了。"
"[english]rd_so_paragraph_drone_3"		"04/20/43, 18:35\nHelvetica's making a lot of sense. I suspect my days with the IAF are numbered. She's promised me a place in the Office- not that she'll tell me what that means. If it's somewhere I can study the swarm with some actual support from command, I'll jump ship in a heartbeat. The only issue is whether to trust when my gut tells me I'm at a global maximum right now. It's possible that any move I make is the wrong one. I can't tell if I'm about to make a deal with the devil, take a life preserver off this sinking ship, or paint a target on my back."
"rd_so_paragraph_drone_4"		"04/20/43, 23:55\n我现在意识到魔鬼可能一只手拿着救生衣，另一只手拿着画笔。"
"[english]rd_so_paragraph_drone_4"		"04/20/43, 23:55\nI now realize the devil may carry a life vest in one hand and a paintbrush in the other."
"rd_so_paragraph_ranger_0"		"太空小子的问题在于，它不断想出新的令人兴奋的方法来杀死你。 它们发明了一种长在腿上的嘴，可以向你喷射酸性物质，最好的防御就是翻跟头。 我们不能不制定了一套系统：其中一个人用杂技和子弹分散注意力，而其他人用棍子击打它。 如果它们知道怎么向上或向下看，我们就得多费些功夫了。 好像这些太空虫子根本不在乎我还有其他工作要做。 你可以告诉它们这些科学箱有地方可去，但它们不会听的。 我都不确定它们有没有耳朵。还是只有腿和嘴。"
"[english]rd_so_paragraph_ranger_0"		"The thing about space is that it keeps coming up with new and exciting ways to kill you. They invented a mouth on legs that spits acid at you and the best defense is a somersault. We had to work out a system where one of us distracts it with acrobatics and bullets while everyone else hits it with a stick. If they ever figure out how to look up or down, it's gonna be a lot more work for us. It's like these space bugs don't even care that I have other work to do. You can tell them these science crates have somewhere to be, but they're not gonna listen. I'm not even sure they have ears. Just legs and a mouth."
"rd_so_paragraph_ranger_1"		"就在前几天，我想去吃太空午餐。 他们有酸球汤、酸球派、酸球披萨，应有尽有。 原来有只虫子在厨房里跑掉了，我们的厨师就好好地物尽其用了。 我不建议这样做——我胃灼热了，且医生一直问我是不是在撒谎。 他们告诉你，你可以翻滚来避开唾沫球，但当它们已经在你体内时，这就不起作用了。 我觉得如果我边喝汤边翻滚，它会更容易向下沉。"
"[english]rd_so_paragraph_ranger_1"		"Just the other day, I was trying to get some space lunch. They had acid orb soup, acid orb pie, acid orb pizza, you name it. Turns out one of these bugs got loose in the kitchen and our chef made the best of it. I don't recommend it- I got nasty heartburn and the doctor kept asking if I was lying. They tell you that you can roll around to avoid the spitballs, but that doesn't work when they're already inside you. I feel like if I had dodgerolled while eating the soup, it would have gone down a lot more easily."
"rd_so_paragraph_ranger_2"		"一些小丑曾经尝试过戏玩酸球，我是第一个觉得这很有趣的，直到他们的手套开始融化。 更有趣的是，他们试图在汤里洗掉它，当它融化在他们的滑稽帽里时就更搞笑了。 这是一个耻辱——他们在小丑战术上做得很好，直到他们决定炫耀。 我想我们都学到了宝贵的一课，当有酸虫四处乱窜时，我们可以扮演小丑：如果你做得对，它可以真的很好。"
"[english]rd_so_paragraph_ranger_2"		"Some clown tried juggling the acid balls once and I'll be the first to admit it was pretty funny until their gloves started to melt. It was even funnier when they tried to wash it off in the soup, and hilarious when it melted right through their horn. It's a shame- they were doing great at the tactical clown rolls until they decided to show off. I like to think we all learned a valuable lesson about clowning around when there's acid bugs scuttling around: it can be really good if you do it right."
"rd_so_paragraph_ranger_3"		"如果有什么安慰的话，那就是它们和其他人一样喜欢睡觉。 我昨晚在我的铺位上发现了一只睡着的虫子，这样更容易让它们躺着睡觉。 当它们蜷成一团，把腿捂在脸上的时，就不会吐那么多口水了。而比被床上的虫子融化还糟糕的是，你用一声枪响把所有虫都吵醒了，它们都对你生气。 老实说，我有过更糟的室友。 它们不会霸占毯子或枕头，还能帮助调节被窝里的温度。 只要确保你在它来之前起床就行了。"
"[english]rd_so_paragraph_ranger_3"		"If there's any consolation, it's that they like to sleep as much as anyone. I found one sleeping in my bunk last night and it was just easier to let sleeping bugs lie. They don't spit so much when they're all curled up with their legs over their face and the only thing worse than getting melted by a bug in your bed is having everyone get mad at you for waking them up with a gunshot. Honestly, I've had worse bunkmates. They don't hog the blankets or pillows and they help regulate the temperature under the covers. Just make sure you get up before it does."
"rd_so_paragraph_ranger_4"		"我开始觉得如果你知道怎么照顾它们就没那么糟了。 正确的饮食，富含碳酸钙和次水杨酸铋，可以大量吸收酸。 频繁的腹部按摩、腿部按摩，每天散步，让虫子报告书在这里也显得很温顺，即使它们仍然试图在我不注意的时候融化皮带。 我想问博士是否有什么手术或基因改造来治疗这种酸，但她只是问我是不是又想做汤，然后笑着把我赶出了房间。 我不知道如何告诉她，她才是能够控制虫子的生成汤速的人。"
"[english]rd_so_paragraph_ranger_4"		"I'm starting to think they're not so bad if you know how to take care of them. The right diet, rich in calcium carbonate and bismuth subsalicylate, can take a lot of bite out of the acid. One day, they'll stop outside and haul me off.\n\nI'm being paranoid, I know. They'll do it while I'm asleep. Less struggle that way. I've signed and sealed my devil's bargain. All that's left to do is wait and see if she delivers. They warned me the devil will be attractive, and that's helping more than I'd like to admit right now. T-minus 12 hours. Time to get everything as ready as I can without broadcasting my intentions. I know they're watching the cameras."
"rd_so_paragraph_shieldbug_4"		"05/05/43，22:20\n成功了。 我仍然惊魂未定，但我做到了。 我已经感到如释重负了。 我不知道的压力开始消失了。 除非这是IAF想要惩罚我的漫长骗局的一部分，否则我自由了。 这种在星际武装部队中步步高升的人是毫无意义的残忍，极其狭隘，而且极其暴怒。 不可否认，这些是老板身上糟糕的特质，但至少是可以预测的。 他们不是那种先假装离开，再端上一杯咖啡来教训别人的人。 \n\n所以，我在这里。 回家自由。 我有我的笔记，我有我的杯子，我有一个我可以信任的人。 顺便说一句，她说的头发是真的。 朱莉，欢迎来到共识维护办公室。"
"[english]rd_so_paragraph_shieldbug_4"		"05/05/43, 22:20\nIt worked. I'm still in shock, but it worked. I can feel the relief already. Stress I didn't know I had is starting to melt off.
